	CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspDatosPrestamo] @nCreditoId INT	
	AS 
	
	DECLARE @t AS TABLE (solicitudID_		INT,
					     nMonto_			NUMERIC(18,2),
					     deslizamiento_		NUMERIC(12,2),
					     fechaInicio_		DATETIME,
					     plazo_				INT, 
					     interes_			NUMERIC(12,2),
					     fechaVence_		DATETIME,
					     frecuencia_		INT,
					     numeroPagos_		INT,
					     tipoCambio_		NUMERIC(12,4),
					     rubro_				VARCHAR(50),
						 fechaUltimoPago	DATETIME)
		
		INSERT INTO @t				
		SELECT T0.nScrSolicitudID,
			   T0.nMontoApruebaC,
			   (SELECT TOP 1 sp.cValorParametro FROM StbParametro AS sp WHERE sp.nCodigoParametro = 150) deslizamiento,
			   T0.dFechaPagado,
			   T0.nPlazoMeses, 
			   T0.nTasaInteres,
			   DATEADD(MONTH,t0.nPlazoMeses,t0.dFechaPagado) vence,
			   T0.frecuencia,
			   T0.NumPagos,
			   T0.nMontoTCambio,
			   T0.rubro,
			   T0.fechaUltimoPago          		   		   		   		   		 		   
		FROM   (
				   SELECT sc.nScrSolicitudID,
						  srd.nTasaInteres, 
						  srd.nComision,
						  sfp.nPlazoMeses frecuencia,
						  srd.nPlazo nPlazoMeses,
						  sfp.nPagosAnios,
						  srd.nPlazo / sfp.nPlazoMeses NumPagos,                					  
						  sm.cDescripcion           moneda,
						  sc.nMontoApruebaC,
						  sd.dFechaPagado,
						  svc.cDescripcion          estado,
						  spc.nMontoTCambio,
						  sr.cDescripcion rubro,
						  (
								SELECT TOP 1 spc2.dFechaPago
								FROM ScrPagoCuota AS spc2
								WHERE spc2.nScrSolicitudID = @nCreditoId
										AND spc2.nActivo = 255
								ORDER BY spc2.dFechaPago DESC										
						  ) fechaUltimoPago
				   FROM   ScrCredito             AS sc
						  JOIN StbCliente        AS sc2
							   ON  sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
						  JOIN StbPersona        AS sp
							   ON  sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
						  JOIN StbRubroDetalle   AS srd
							   ON  srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
						  JOIN StbRubro          AS sr
							   ON  sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
						  JOIN StbFrecuenciaPagos AS sfp
							   ON  sfp.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID = srd.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID
						  JOIN StbMoneda         AS sm
							   ON  sm.nStbMonedaID = sc.nStbMonedaID
						  JOIN StbValorCatalogo  AS svc
							   ON  sc.nStbEstadoSolicitudID = svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
						  JOIN ScrDesembolso AS sd
							   ON sd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
						  JOIN StbParidadCambiaria AS spc
							   ON sd.nStbParidadCambiariaID = spc.nStbParidadCambiariaID						 
				   WHERE  svc.cCodigoInterno = '7'
						  AND sc.nScrSolicitudID = @nCreditoId
		) T0		
		
SELECT * FROM @t		   	

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspGeneraNumeroCredito]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspGeneraNumeroCredito]
AS

DECLARE @numeroSolicitud INT,
		@numeroSolicitudLen INT

SELECT    TOP 1  @numeroSolicitud = cast(nNumeroSolicitud AS INT)
FROM      ScrCredito AS sc
ORDER BY  cast(nNumeroSolicitud AS INT) DESC


SELECT CASE WHEN @numeroSolicitud IS NULL THEN '000001'
				 ELSE RIGHT('000000',6-LEN(CONVERT(varchar(10), @numeroSolicitud))) + (CONVERT(VARCHAR(10),(@numeroSolicitud + 1)))
				 END campo
				 		

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspGeneraNumeroPagoCuota]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspGeneraNumeroPagoCuota]
AS

DECLARE @numeroPago INT		

SELECT    TOP 1  @numeroPago = sc.cNumeroDocumento
FROM      ScrPagoCuota AS sc
ORDER BY  sc.cNumeroDocumento DESC


SELECT CASE WHEN @numeroPago IS NULL THEN '000001'
				 ELSE RIGHT('000000',6-LEN(CONVERT(varchar(10), @numeroPago))) + (CONVERT(VARCHAR(10),(@numeroPago + 1)))
				 END campo
				 		

GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspRptDetalleCuotaCalculoDiario]		@N_CREDITO_ID		INT,
												@N_CUAOTA_ID		INT

AS

SET NOCOUNT ON 

--SET @N_CREDITO_ID	= 1030
--SET @N_CUAOTA_ID	= 4487

SELECT ISNULL(T0.nScrSolicitudID, 0)								nScrSolicitudID,
       ISNULL(T0.cliente, '')										cliente,
       ISNULL(T0.nTasaInteres, 0)									nTasaInteres,
       ISNULL(T0.nComision, 0)										nComision,
       ISNULL(T0.frecuencia, 0)										frecuencia,
       ISNULL(T0.nPlazoMeses, 0)									nPlazoMeses,
       ISNULL(T0.nPagosAnios, 0)									nPagosAnios,
       ISNULL(T0.NumPagos, 0)										NumPagos,
       ISNULL(T0.moneda, '')										moneda,
       ISNULL(T0.nMontoApruebaC, 0)									nMontoApruebaC,
       ISNULL(T0.dFechaPagado, '01/01/2999')						dFechaPagado,
       ISNULL(T0.estado, '')										estado,
       ISNULL(T0.nMontoTCambio, 0)									nMontoTCambio,
       ISNULL(T0.rubro, '')											rubro,
       ISNULL(T0.proceso, '')										proceso,
       ISNULL(T0.dFecha, '01/01/2999')								dFecha,
       ISNULL(T0.nTipoCambio, 0)									nTipoCambio,
       ISNULL(T0.nMontoEntregado, 0)								nMontoEntregado,
       ISNULL(T0.nMmtoValor, 0)										nMmtoValor,
       ISNULL(T0.nAmortizacionPrincipal, 0)							nAmortizacionPrincipal,
       ISNULL(T0.nMontoAcumuladoAntes, 0)							nMontoAcumuladoAntes,
       ISNULL(T0.nMontoAcumulado, 0)								nMontoAcumulado,
       ISNULL(T0.dFechaDesde, '01/01/2999')							dFechaDesde,
       ISNULL(T0.dFechaHasta, '01/01/2999')							dFechaHasta,
       ISNULL(T0.nDias, 0)											nDias,
       ISNULL(T0.nInteresCorriente, 0)								nInteresCorriente,
       ISNULL(T0.nMoratorios, 0)									nMoratorios,
       ISNULL(T0.nMmtoInteres, 0)									nMmtoInteres,
       ISNULL(T0.nAmortizacionInteres, 0)							nAmortizacionInteres,
       ISNULL(T0.nInteresAcumulado, 0)								nInteresAcumulado,
       ISNULL(T0.nSaldoTotal, 0)									nSaldoTotal,
       ISNULL(T0.nFuenteSaldos, '')									nFuenteSaldos,
       ISNULL(T0.nEstado, 0)										nEstado,
       ISNULL(T0.nScrPagoCuotaID, 0)								nScrPagoCuotaID
FROM 
(
SELECT sc.nScrSolicitudID,
       ISNULL(sp.cNombre1, ' ') + ' ' +
       ISNULL(sp.cNombre2, ' ') + ' ' +
       ISNULL(sp.cApellido1, ' ') + ' ' +
       ISNULL(sp.cApellido2, ' ')						cliente,       
       srd.nTasaInteres,
       srd.nComision,
       cast(sfp.nPlazoMeses AS SMALLINT)                frecuencia,
       cast(srd.nPlazo AS SMALLINT)						nPlazoMeses,
       cast(sfp.nPagosAnios AS SMALLINT)				nPagosAnios,
       cast((srd.nPlazo / sfp.nPlazoMeses) AS SMALLINT)	NumPagos,
       sm.cDescripcion									moneda,
       sc.nMontoApruebaC,
       sd.dFechaPagado,
       svc.cDescripcion									estado,
       spc.nMontoTCambio,
       sr.cDescripcion									rubro,
       
       ------------------------------------------------
       
       sfcb.proceso,
       sfcb.dFecha,
       sfcb.nTipoCambio,
       sfcb.nMontoEntregado,
       sfcb.nMmtoValor,
       sfcb.nAmortizacionPrincipal,
       sfcb.nMontoAcumuladoAntes,
       sfcb.nMontoAcumulado,
       sfcb.dFechaDesde,
       sfcb.dFechaHasta,
       sfcb.nDias,
       sfcb.nInteresCorriente,
       sfcb.nMoratorios,
       sfcb.nMmtoInteres,
       sfcb.nAmortizacionInteres,
       sfcb.nInteresAcumulado,
       sfcb.nSaldoTotal,
       sfcb.nFuenteSaldos,
       cast(sfcb.nEstado AS SMALLINT)					nEstado,
       sfcb.nScrPagoCuotaID
		
	   ------------------------------------------------
		
FROM ScrFormatoCalculoBimensual AS sfcb
	JOIN ScrCredito AS sc
		ON sfcb.creditoid = sc.nScrSolicitudID
	JOIN StbCliente AS sc2
		ON sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
	JOIN StbPersona AS sp
		ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
	JOIN StbRubroDetalle   AS srd
		ON  srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
	JOIN StbRubro          AS sr
		ON  sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
	JOIN StbFrecuenciaPagos AS sfp
		ON  sfp.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID = srd.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID
	JOIN StbMoneda         AS sm
		ON  sm.nStbMonedaID = sc.nStbMonedaID
	JOIN StbValorCatalogo  AS svc
		ON  sc.nStbEstadoSolicitudID = svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
	JOIN ScrDesembolso AS sd
		ON sd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
	JOIN StbParidadCambiaria AS spc
		ON sd.nStbParidadCambiariaID = spc.nStbParidadCambiariaID 
WHERE sc.nScrSolicitudID			= @N_CREDITO_ID		
		AND sfcb.nScrPagoCuotaID	<= @N_CUAOTA_ID
--ORDER BY sfcb.dFecha		
) T0
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspRptDetallePagosControlPrestamo]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO

GO



CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspRptDetallePagosControlPrestamo] @N_CREDITO_ID INT
AS

SELECT sc.nScrSolicitudID			NSCRSOLICITUDID,
		sc.nStbClienteID			NSTBCLIENTEID,
		sp.cNombre1					CNOMBRE1, 
		sp.cNombre2					CNOMBRE2, 
		sp.cApellido1				CAPELLIDO1, 
		sp.cApellido2				CAPELLIDO2,
		sc.nMontoApruebaC			NMONTOAPRUEBAC,
		sd.dFechaPagado				DFECHAPAGADO,		
		spc.dFechaPago				DFECHAPAGO,
		sr.cDescripcion				RUBRO,
		srd.nTasaInteres			NTASAINTERES, 
		srd.nPlazo					NPLAZO,
		sfp.nPlazoMeses				NPLAZOMESES, 
		sfp.nPagosAnios				APAGOSANIOS,
		stcp.N_INDICE, 
		stcp.D_FECHA_CORTE,
		stcp.N_PAGO_ID,
		stcp.N_TIPO_CAMBIO, 		
		sc.nMontoApruebaC			NMONTOAPRUEBAC,
		stcp.N_MANTENIMIENTO_DEVENGADO_AM,
		stcp.N_MANTENIMIENTO_ABONADO_AM,
		stcp.N_AMORTIZACION_ABONADA, 
		stcp.N_DESEMBOLSO_ACTUALIZADO,
		stcp.N_DIAS_ENTRE_FECHA,
		stcp.N_INTERES_DEVENGADO N_INTERES_DEVENGADO_ACUMULADO,
		--stcp.N_INTERES_DEVENGADO_ACUMULADO,
		--stcp.N_INTERES_PENDIENTE, 		
		stcp.N_INTERES_ABONADO,		
		stcp.N_SALDO_TOTAL,
		STCP.N_MONTO_PAGO
FROM ScrTablaControlPrestamo AS stcp
	JOIN ScrPagoCuota AS spc
		ON stcp.N_PAGO_ID = spc.nScrPagoCuotaID
	JOIN ScrPagoCuotaDetalle AS spcd
		ON spcd.nScrPagoCuotaID = spc.nScrPagoCuotaID
	JOIN ScrCredito AS sc
		ON sc.nScrSolicitudID = spc.nScrSolicitudID
	JOIN StbCliente AS sc2
		ON sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
	JOIN StbPersona AS sp
		ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
	JOIN StbRubroDetalle AS srd
		ON srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
	JOIN StbRubro AS sr
		ON sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
	JOIN ScrDesembolso AS sd
		ON sd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
	JOIN StbFrecuenciaPagos AS sfp
		ON sfp.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID = srd.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID
WHERE sc.nScrSolicitudID = @N_CREDITO_ID		
GROUP BY sc.nScrSolicitudID,
		sc.nStbClienteID,
		sp.cNombre1, 
		sp.cNombre2, 
		sp.cApellido1, 
		sp.cApellido2,
		sc.nMontoApruebaC,
		sd.dFechaPagado,		
		spc.dFechaPago,
		sr.cDescripcion,
		srd.nTasaInteres, 
		srd.nPlazo,
		sfp.nPlazoMeses, 
		sfp.nPagosAnios,
		stcp.N_INDICE, 
		stcp.D_FECHA_CORTE,
		stcp.N_PAGO_ID,
		stcp.N_TIPO_CAMBIO, 		
		sc.nMontoApruebaC,
		stcp.N_MANTENIMIENTO_DEVENGADO_AM,
		stcp.N_MANTENIMIENTO_ABONADO_AM,
		stcp.N_AMORTIZACION_ABONADA, 
		stcp.N_DESEMBOLSO_ACTUALIZADO,
		stcp.N_DIAS_ENTRE_FECHA,
		stcp.N_INTERES_DEVENGADO,
		--stcp.N_INTERES_DEVENGADO_ACUMULADO,
		--stcp.N_INTERES_PENDIENTE, 		
		stcp.N_INTERES_ABONADO,		
		stcp.N_SALDO_TOTAL,
		STCP.N_MONTO_PAGO		




GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspRptEgresosRangoFechas]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspRptEgresosRangoFechas] @FECHAINICIO DATETIME,
											@FECHAFIN DATETIME,
											@FONDOID INT,
											@RUBROID INT,
											@COMARCAID INT
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

--SET @FECHAINICIO = '20161101'
--SET @FECHAFIN = '20161130'


DECLARE @tabla AS TABLE(SOLICITUDID INT,
					    CLIENTEID INT,
					    DESEMBOLSOID INT,
					    CLIENTE VARCHAR(200),					    
					    MONTOCOR NUMERIC(18,2),
					    MONTOUSD NUMERIC(18,2),
					    RUBRO VARCHAR(50),
					    TIPOCAMBIO NUMERIC(8,4),
						FONDOID INT,
						RUBROID INT,
						COMARCAID INT,
						FONDO VARCHAR(50),
						COMARCA VARCHAR(30))


INSERT INTO @tabla(SOLICITUDID, 
					CLIENTEID, 
					DESEMBOLSOID, 
					CLIENTE, 
					MONTOCOR,
					MONTOUSD, 
					RUBRO, 
					TIPOCAMBIO, 
					FONDOID, 
					RUBROID, 
					COMARCAID, 
					FONDO,
					COMARCA)

SELECT      sc.nScrSolicitudID					SOLICITUDID, 
			sc.nStbClienteID					CLIENTEID,
			SD.nScrDesembolsoID					DESEMBOLSOID,
			isnull(sp.cNombre1,'') + ' ' + 
			isnull(sp.cNombre2,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido1,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido2,'')			CLIENTE, 
			sc.nMontoApruebaC					MONTOCOR, 
			sc.nMontoApruebaU					MONTOUSD,			
			sr.cDescripcion						RUBRO,
			spc.nMontoTCambio					TIPOCAMBIO,
			sc.nStbFondoId,
			srd.nStbRubroID,
			sp.nStbBarrioComarcaID,
			svc.cDescripcion					FONDO,
			sbc.cNombreComarca					COMARCA
						
			
FROM	ScrCredito AS sc
			JOIN StbCliente AS sc2
				ON sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
			JOIN StbPersona AS sp
				ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
			JOIN ScrDesembolso AS sd
				ON sd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
			JOIN StbRubroDetalle AS srd
				ON srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
			JOIN StbRubro AS sr
				ON sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
			JOIN StbParidadCambiaria AS spc
				ON spc.nStbParidadCambiariaID = sd.nStbParidadCambiariaID
			JOIN StbValorCatalogo AS svc
				ON svc.nStbValorCatalogoID = sc.nStbFondoId
			JOIN StbBarrioComarca AS sbc
				ON SP.nStbBarrioComarcaID = SBC.nStbComarcaID
WHERE		sc.nStbEstadoSolicitudID IN 
														(
															SELECT svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
															FROM StbValorCatalogo AS svc
															WHERE svc.nStbCatalogoID IN 
																	(
																		SELECT sc.nStbCatalogoID
																		FROM	StbCatalogo AS sc
																		WHERE sc.cNombre = 'EstadoSolicitudPrestamo'
																	) AND svc.cCodigoInterno IN ('7')	
														)	
			/*sd.nStbEstadoDesembolsoID = 
										(
											SELECT svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
											FROM StbValorCatalogo AS svc
											WHERE svc.nStbCatalogoID IN 
													(
														SELECT sc.nStbCatalogoID
														FROM	StbCatalogo AS sc
														WHERE sc.cNombre = 'EstadoPagoDesembolso'
													) AND svc.cCodigoInterno = '04'	
										)*/
			AND sd.dFechaDesembolso BETWEEN (@FECHAINICIO) AND (@FECHAFIN)																	

IF @FONDOID > 0
BEGIN		
	DELETE FROM @tabla WHERE FONDOID NOT IN (@FONDOID)	
END

IF @RUBROID > 0 
BEGIN
	DELETE FROM @tabla WHERE RUBROID NOT IN (@RUBROID) 
END

IF @COMARCAID > 0
BEGIN
	DELETE FROM @tabla WHERE COMARCAID NOT IN (@COMARCAID)
END

---salida
SELECT * FROM @tabla			

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspRptResumenIngresosRangoFechas]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspRptResumenIngresosRangoFechas] @FECHAINICIA DATETIME,
													@FECHAFIN DATETIME,
													@FONDOID INT,
													@RUBROID INT,
													@COMARCAID INT
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

--SET @FECHAINICIA = '20161101'
--SET @FECHAFIN = '20161129'

DECLARE @tabla AS TABLE(FECHAPAGO DATETIME,
					    NORECIBO VARCHAR(10),
					    RUBRO VARCHAR(200),					    
					    TIPOCAMBIO NUMERIC(18,2),
					    SOLICITUDID NUMERIC(18,2),
					    CLIENTEID DATETIME,
					    CLIENTE DATETIME,
					    PRINCIPALCOR NUMERIC(18,2),
					    MMTOCOR NUMERIC(18,2),
					    INTERESCOR NUMERIC(18,2),
					    TOTALCOR NUMERIC(18,2),
					    PRINCIPALDOL NUMERIC(18,2),
					    MMTODOL NUMERIC(18,2),
					    INTERESDOL NUMERIC(18,2),
					    TOTALDOL NUMERIC(18,2),
						FONDOID INT,
						RUBROID INT,
						COMARCAID INT)

INSERT INTO @tabla(FECHAPAGO, 
				   NORECIBO, 
				   RUBRO, 
				   TIPOCAMBIO, 
				   SOLICITUDID, 
				   CLIENTEID,
				   CLIENTE, 
				   PRINCIPALCOR, 
				   MMTOCOR, 
				   INTERESCOR, 
				   TOTALCOR, 
				   PRINCIPALDOL,
				   MMTODOL, 
				   INTERESDOL, 
				   TOTALDOL, 
				   FONDOID, 
				   RUBROID, 
				   COMARCAID)

SELECT      spc.dFechaPago													FECHAPAGO,
			spc.cNumeroDocumento											NORECIBO,
			sr.cDescripcion													RUBRO,
			spc2.nMontoTCambio												TIPOCAMBIO,
			sc.nScrSolicitudID												SOLICITUDID, 
			sc.nStbClienteID												CLIENTEID,
			isnull(sp.cNombre1,'') + ' ' + 
			isnull(sp.cNombre2,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido1,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido2,'')										CLIENTE, 
			
			sum(spcd.nMontoPrincipal)										PRINCIPALCOR,
			SUM(spcd.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal + 
				spcd.nMontoMantenimientoInteres)							MMTOCOR,
			SUM(spcd.nMontoInteres)											INTERESCOR,
			
			SUM(spcd.nMontoPrincipal +										
				spcd.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal + 
				spcd.nMontoMantenimientoInteres +							
			    spcd.nMontoInteres)											TOTALCOR,
			
			sum(spcd.nMontoPrincipal / spc2.nMontoTCambio)					PRINCIPALDOL,
			(SUM(spcd.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal + 
				spcd.nMontoMantenimientoInteres)) / spc2.nMontoTCambio		MMTODOL,
			SUM(spcd.nMontoInteres) / spc2.nMontoTCambio					INTERESDOL,
			
			(SUM(spcd.nMontoPrincipal +										
				spcd.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal + 
				spcd.nMontoMantenimientoInteres +							
			    spcd.nMontoInteres)) / spc2.nMontoTCambio					TOTALDOL,
			isnull(sc.nStbFondoId,0) nStbFondoId,
			isnull(srd.nStbRubroID,0) nStbRubroID,
			isnull(sp.nStbBarrioComarcaID,0) nStbBarrioComarcaID
									
FROM	ScrCredito AS sc
			JOIN StbCliente AS sc2
				ON sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
			JOIN StbPersona AS sp
				ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
			JOIN ScrPagoCuota AS spc
				ON spc.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
			JOIN ScrPagoCuotaDetalle AS spcd
				ON spcd.nScrPagoCuotaID = spc.nScrPagoCuotaID
			JOIN StbRubroDetalle AS srd
				ON srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
			JOIN StbRubro AS sr
				ON sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
			JOIN StbParidadCambiaria AS spc2
				ON spc2.nStbParidadCambiariaID = spc.nStbParidadCambiariaID
WHERE		spc.nActivo = 255
			AND spc.dFechaPago BETWEEN (@FECHAINICIA) AND (@FECHAFIN)										
													
GROUP BY 	spc.dFechaPago,
			spc.cNumeroDocumento,
			sr.cDescripcion,													
			spc2.nMontoTCambio,												
			sc.nScrSolicitudID,											 
			sc.nStbClienteID,
			isnull(sp.cNombre1,'') + ' ' + 
			isnull(sp.cNombre2,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido1,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido2,''),
			sc.nStbFondoId,
			srd.nStbRubroID,
			sp.nStbBarrioComarcaID	


IF @FONDOID > 0
BEGIN		
	DELETE FROM @tabla WHERE FONDOID NOT IN (@FONDOID)	
END

IF @RUBROID > 0 
BEGIN
	DELETE FROM @tabla WHERE RUBROID NOT IN (@RUBROID) 
END

IF @COMARCAID > 0
BEGIN
	DELETE FROM @tabla WHERE COMARCAID NOT IN (@COMARCAID)
END

---salida
SELECT * FROM @tabla			
	

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspRptTablaProyeccionPagos]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspRptTablaProyeccionPagos] @CREDITOID INT
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

DECLARE @DESLIZAMIENTO	NUMERIC(12,2)

SELECT  @DESLIZAMIENTO = convert(numeric(8,2),sp.cValorParametro)
FROM    StbParametro AS sp
WHERE	sp.nCodigoParametro = 150


SELECT      sc.nScrSolicitudID							SOLICITUDID, 
			sc.nStbClienteID							CLIENTEID,
			isnull(sp.cNombre1,'') + ' ' + 
			isnull(sp.cNombre2,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido1,'') + ' '  + 
			isnull(sp.cApellido2,'')					CLIENTE, 
			sc.nMontoApruebaC							MONTOCOR, 
			sc.nMontoApruebaU							MONTOUSD,			
			srd.nTasaInteres							TASAINTERES,
			srd.nPlazo									PLAZO,
			srd.nPlazo / sfp.nPlazoMeses				NUMPAGOS,
			sfp.cDescripcion							FRECUENCIA,						
			sd.dFechaPagado								FECHAENTREGA,			
			DATEADD(MONTH,srd.nPlazo,sd.dFechaPagado)	FECHAVENCE,	
			spc.nMontoTCambio							TIPOCAMBIO,	
			@DESLIZAMIENTO								PORDELIZAMIENTO,
			stp.nNumeroCuota							NOCUOTA,													
			stp.dFechaPago								FECHAPAGO,
			stp.nMontoPrincipal							PRINCIPAL,
			stp.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal			MMTO,
			stp.nMontoInteres							MONTOINTERES,
			stp.nMontoTotal								TOTAL,
			stp.nMontoSaldo								SALDO				
			
			
FROM	ScrCredito AS sc
			JOIN StbCliente AS sc2
				ON sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
			JOIN StbPersona AS sp
				ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
			JOIN ScrDesembolso AS sd
				ON sd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID			
			JOIN StbRubroDetalle AS srd
				ON srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
			JOIN StbRubro AS sr
				ON sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
			JOIN StbFrecuenciaPagos AS sfp
				ON sfp.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID = srd.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID
			JOIN ScrTablaproyeccionPago AS stp
				ON stp.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
			JOIN StbParidadCambiaria AS spc
				ON spc.nStbParidadCambiariaID = sc.nStbParidadCambiariaID
WHERE		sc.nScrSolicitudID = @CREDITOID				
				
				
																			
		



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScDatosCreditoCliente]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/

CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScDatosCreditoCliente] @CREDITOID INT 
AS

SELECT  sc.nScrSolicitudID, 
		sc.nStbClienteID,
		sc2.cCodigoCliente,
		sp.cNombre1,
        sp.cNombre2, 
        sp.cApellido1, 
        sp.cApellido2,
        svc.cDescripcion estado,
        -----------------------------rubro
        sr.cDescripcion rubro,
        srd.nPlazo,
        srd.nTasaInteres,
        sfp.nPlazoMeses,         
        sfp.cDescripcion frecuencia,
        -----------------------------desembolso
        sd.dFechaDesembolso, 
        sd.nMontoDesembolso, 
        sd.nPorcentajeComision,
        sd.nMontoComsion, 
        sd.nMontoTotal
FROM ScrCredito AS sc
	JOIN StbCliente AS sc2
		ON sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
	JOIN StbPersona AS sp
		ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
	JOIN StbValorCatalogo AS svc
		ON svc.nStbValorCatalogoID = sc.nStbEstadoSolicitudID
	LEFT JOIN ScrDesembolso AS sd
		ON sd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
	JOIN StbRubroDetalle AS srd
		ON srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
	JOIN StbRubro AS sr
		ON sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
	JOIN StbFrecuenciaPagos AS sfp
		ON sfp.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID = srd.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID
WHERE sc.nScrSolicitudID = @CREDITOID		
		
		
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrAccionesAplicacionModuloServicio]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrAccionesAplicacionModuloServicio] 
			@aplicacionId INT, 			 
			@rolId INT,
			@todos TINYINT
AS 

IF @todos = 0
BEGIN
	
	SELECT sm.Nombre                AS modulo_,
		   ssu.Nombre				AS Servicio_,
           sa.Nombre				AS accion_,
           sa.SsgAccionID			AS accionId_
	FROM SsgAccion AS sa
			JOIN SsgServicioUsuario  AS ssu
				ON ssu.SsgServicioUsuarioID = sa.objServicioUsuarioID		
		   INNER JOIN SsgModulo           AS sm
				ON  sm.SsgModuloID = ssu.objModuloID	
	ORDER BY
		   sm.Nombre,
		   ssu.Nombre,
		   sa.Nombre	       		
END

IF @todos = 255
BEGIN
	
	SELECT sm.Nombre                      AS modulo_,
		   ssu.Nombre                     AS servicio_,
		   sa.Nombre                      AS accion_,
		   sa.SsgAccionID				  AS accionId_	   
	FROM   SsgRolAccion
		   INNER JOIN SsgRol
				ON  SsgRolAccion.objRolID    = SsgRol.SsgRolID
		   INNER JOIN SsgAccion           AS sa
				ON  SsgRolAccion.objAccionID = sa.SsgAccionID
		   INNER JOIN SsgServicioUsuario  AS ssu
				ON  ssu.SsgServicioUsuarioID = sa.objServicioUsuarioID
		   INNER JOIN SsgModulo           AS sm
				ON  sm.SsgModuloID = ssu.objModuloID
	WHERE  SsgRol.SsgRolID = @rolId
		   AND sm.objAplicacionID  = @aplicacionId				
	ORDER BY
		   sm.Nombre,
		   ssu.Nombre,
		   sa.Nombre
	
END
				
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrActualizaEstadoCuotasTablaProyeccion]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


/************************************************************
 * Code formatted by SoftTree SQL Assistant © v6.5.278
 * Time: 18/05/2017 11:52:24
 ************************************************************/


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrActualizaEstadoCuotasTablaProyeccion]
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON


BEGIN TRY
	
	--1: CUOTAS VENCIDAS
	IF EXISTS(SELECT  nScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamicaID
			  FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica 
			  WHERE  dFechaPago < CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CONVERT(DATETIME, GETDATE(), 103), 112)
				AND cEstadoPago NOT IN ('PA', 'VE'))
	BEGIN
		UPDATE ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica
		SET    cEstadoPago = 'VE'
		WHERE  dFechaPago < CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CONVERT(DATETIME, GETDATE(), 103), 112)
			   AND cEstadoPago NOT IN ('PA', 'VE')		
	END
	--ELSE
	--	RETURN;
	-----------------------------------------------
	--2: CUOTAS VIGENTES
	DECLARE @T AS TABLE (INDICE INT NULL, CREDITOID INT NULL)
	DECLARE @N_MIN INT
	DECLARE @N_MAX INT	
	DECLARE @N_CUOTA INT
	DECLARE @N_CREDITO_ID INT 
	
	-- INSERTO LOS CREDITOS DE CUOTAS PENDIENTES DE LA TABLA DINAMICA.
	INSERT INTO @T
	  (
	    INDICE,
	    CREDITOID
	  )
	--SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY stpd.nScrSolicitudID),
	--       stpd.nScrSolicitudID
	--FROM   ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
	--WHERE  stpd.cEstadoPago = 'PE'
	--GROUP BY
	--       stpd.nScrSolicitudID 
	
	SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY T.nScrSolicitudID), 
		   T.nScrSolicitudID
	FROM
	(
		SELECT DISTINCT stpd.nScrSolicitudID
		FROM ScrCredito AS sc
				JOIN ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
					ON stpd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
		WHERE sc.nStbEstadoSolicitudID = (
											SELECT svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
											FROM StbValorCatalogo AS svc
													JOIN StbCatalogo AS sc2
														ON sc2.nStbCatalogoID = svc.nStbCatalogoID
											WHERE sc2.cNombre = 'EstadoSolicitudPrestamo'
													AND svc.cCodigoInterno = '7'
										 )	
				AND stpd.cEstadoPago NOT IN ('VE', 'PA')
	)T									 			
	
	--SI HAY CUOTAS PENDIENTES
	IF (
	       SELECT COUNT(*)
	       FROM   @T
	   ) > 0
	BEGIN
	    ------- INDICES MAXIMO Y MINIMO -------
	    SELECT TOP 1 @N_MIN = INDICE
	    FROM   @T
	    ORDER BY INDICE
	    
	    SELECT TOP 1 @N_MAX = INDICE
	    FROM   @T
	    ORDER BY INDICE DESC
	    
	    WHILE (@N_MIN <= @N_MAX)
	    BEGIN	    			
	    	
	    	--VERIFICO SI HAY CREDITOS SIN CUOTA VIGENTE	    	
	    	IF (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT stpd.cEstadoPago)
	    	    FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
	    	    WHERE stpd.nScrSolicitudID = (
												SELECT CREDITOID
												FROM   @T
												WHERE  INDICE = @N_MIN)
					AND stpd.cEstadoPago NOT IN ('VE', 'PA')
	    	) = 1
	    	
	    	BEGIN
	    		
	    		--OBTENGO LA PRIMERA CUOTA PENDIENTE DEL CREDITO
				SELECT TOP 1 @N_CREDITO_ID = stpd.nScrSolicitudID,
							 @N_CUOTA = stpd.nNumeroCuota
				FROM   ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
				WHERE  stpd.nScrSolicitudID = (
						   SELECT CREDITOID
						   FROM   @T
						   WHERE  INDICE = @N_MIN
					   )	
					   AND stpd.cEstadoPago NOT IN ('VE', 'PA')				   
				ORDER BY stpd.nNumeroCuota 
	        
				--ACTUALIZO A ESTADO VIGENTE
				UPDATE ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica
				SET    cEstadoPago = 'VI'
				WHERE  nScrSolicitudID = @N_CREDITO_ID
					   AND nNumeroCuota = @N_CUOTA
	    		
	    	END
	    		        	        
	        SET @N_MIN += 1
	    END

		--ACTUALIZO CUOTAS DE TABLA DE PAGOS PRINCIPAL
		UPDATE pp
		SET    pp.cEstadoPago = ppd.cEstadoPago
		FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPago pp,  ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica ppd
		WHERE pp.nScrSolicitudID = ppd.nScrSolicitudID 
			AND pp.nNumeroCuota = ppd.nNumeroCuota  
				

	END
END TRY
BEGIN CATCH
	
	INSERT INTO StbErrorresLog(OBJETO, 
							   ERRORNUMBER, 
							   ERRORSEVERITY, 
							   ERRORSTATES,
							   ERRORPROCC, 
							   ERRORLINE, 
							   ERRORMESSG) 
	SELECT
	'uspScrActualizaEstadoCuotasTablaProyeccion',
	ERROR_NUMBER() AS ErrorNumber,
	ERROR_SEVERITY() AS ErrorSeverity,
	ERROR_STATE() AS ErrorState,
	ERROR_PROCEDURE() AS ErrorProcedure,
	ERROR_LINE() AS ErrorLine,
	ERROR_MESSAGE() AS ErrorMessage
	
END CATCH





GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrActualizaEstadoCuotasTablaProyeccionPrestamoId]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


--SELECT * FROM ScrCredito AS sc WHERE sc.dFechaAprobacion >= '20190501'
--SELECT * FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPago AS stp WHERE stp.nScrSolicitudID = 11205 stp.cEstadoPago IN ('VI','PE') ORDER BY stp.nScrSolicitudID

/************************************************************
 * Code formatted by SoftTree SQL Assistant © v6.5.278
 * Time: 18/05/2017 11:52:24
 ************************************************************/
 

CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrActualizaEstadoCuotasTablaProyeccionPrestamoId] @nScrSolicitudID	INT
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON


BEGIN TRY
	
	--1: CUOTAS VENCIDAS
	IF EXISTS(SELECT  nScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamicaID
			  FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica 
			  WHERE  dFechaPago < CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CONVERT(DATETIME, GETDATE(), 103), 112)
				AND cEstadoPago NOT IN ('PA', 'VE')
				AND nScrSolicitudID = @nScrSolicitudID)
				
	BEGIN
		UPDATE ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica
		SET    cEstadoPago = 'VE'
		WHERE  dFechaPago < CONVERT(VARCHAR(10), CONVERT(DATETIME, GETDATE(), 103), 112)
			   AND cEstadoPago NOT IN ('PA', 'VE')		
			   AND nScrSolicitudID = @nScrSolicitudID
	END
	--ELSE
	--	RETURN;
	-----------------------------------------------
	--2: CUOTAS VIGENTES
	DECLARE @T AS TABLE (INDICE INT NULL, CREDITOID INT NULL)
	DECLARE @N_MIN INT
	DECLARE @N_MAX INT	
	DECLARE @N_CUOTA INT
	DECLARE @N_CREDITO_ID INT 
	
	-- INSERTO LOS CREDITOS DE CUOTAS PENDIENTES DE LA TABLA DINAMICA.
	INSERT INTO @T
	  (
	    INDICE,
	    CREDITOID
	  )
	--SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY stpd.nScrSolicitudID),
	--       stpd.nScrSolicitudID
	--FROM   ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
	--WHERE  stpd.cEstadoPago = 'PE'
	--GROUP BY
	--       stpd.nScrSolicitudID 
	
	SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER(ORDER BY T.nScrSolicitudID), 
		   T.nScrSolicitudID
	FROM
	(
		SELECT DISTINCT stpd.nScrSolicitudID
		FROM ScrCredito AS sc
				JOIN ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
					ON stpd.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
		WHERE sc.nStbEstadoSolicitudID = (
											SELECT svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
											FROM StbValorCatalogo AS svc
													JOIN StbCatalogo AS sc2
														ON sc2.nStbCatalogoID = svc.nStbCatalogoID
											WHERE sc2.cNombre = 'EstadoSolicitudPrestamo'
													AND svc.cCodigoInterno = '7'
										 )	
				AND stpd.cEstadoPago NOT IN ('VE', 'PA')
				AND stpd.nScrSolicitudID = @nScrSolicitudID
	)T									 			
	
	--SI HAY CUOTAS PENDIENTES
	IF (
	       SELECT COUNT(*)
	       FROM   @T
	   ) > 0
	BEGIN
	    ------- INDICES MAXIMO Y MINIMO -------
	    SELECT TOP 1 @N_MIN = INDICE
	    FROM   @T
	    ORDER BY INDICE
	    
	    SELECT TOP 1 @N_MAX = INDICE
	    FROM   @T
	    ORDER BY INDICE DESC
	    
	    WHILE (@N_MIN <= @N_MAX)
	    BEGIN	    			
	    	
	    	--VERIFICO SI HAY CREDITOS SIN CUOTA VIGENTE	    	
	    	IF (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT stpd.cEstadoPago)
	    	    FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
	    	    WHERE stpd.nScrSolicitudID = (
												SELECT CREDITOID
												FROM   @T
												WHERE  INDICE = @N_MIN)
					AND stpd.cEstadoPago NOT IN ('VE', 'PA')
					AND stpd.nScrSolicitudID = @nScrSolicitudID
	    	) = 1
	    	
	    	BEGIN
	    		
	    		--OBTENGO LA PRIMERA CUOTA PENDIENTE DEL CREDITO
				SELECT TOP 1 @N_CREDITO_ID = stpd.nScrSolicitudID,
							 @N_CUOTA = stpd.nNumeroCuota
				FROM   ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stpd
				WHERE  stpd.nScrSolicitudID = (
						   SELECT CREDITOID
						   FROM   @T
						   WHERE  INDICE = @N_MIN
					   )	
					   AND stpd.cEstadoPago NOT IN ('VE', 'PA')		
					   AND stpd.nScrSolicitudID = @nScrSolicitudID		   
				ORDER BY stpd.nNumeroCuota 
	        
				--ACTUALIZO A ESTADO VIGENTE
				UPDATE ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica
				SET    cEstadoPago = 'VI'
				WHERE  nScrSolicitudID = @N_CREDITO_ID
					   AND nNumeroCuota = @N_CUOTA
	    		
	    	END
	    		        	        
	        SET @N_MIN += 1
	    END

		--ACTUALIZO CUOTAS DE TABLA DE PAGOS PRINCIPAL
		UPDATE pp
		SET    pp.cEstadoPago = ppd.cEstadoPago
		FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPago pp,  ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica ppd
		WHERE pp.nScrSolicitudID = ppd.nScrSolicitudID 
			AND pp.nNumeroCuota = ppd.nNumeroCuota  
				

	END
END TRY
BEGIN CATCH
	
	INSERT INTO StbErrorresLog(OBJETO, 
							   ERRORNUMBER, 
							   ERRORSEVERITY, 
							   ERRORSTATES,
							   ERRORPROCC, 
							   ERRORLINE, 
							   ERRORMESSG) 
	SELECT
	'uspScrActualizaEstadoCuotasTablaProyeccion',
	ERROR_NUMBER() AS ErrorNumber,
	ERROR_SEVERITY() AS ErrorSeverity,
	ERROR_STATE() AS ErrorState,
	ERROR_PROCEDURE() AS ErrorProcedure,
	ERROR_LINE() AS ErrorLine,
	ERROR_MESSAGE() AS ErrorMessage
	
END CATCH





GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrAnulaCredito]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrAnulaCredito] @creditoID INT
AS

DECLARE @estado INT,
		@result BIT

BEGIN
	
	SELECT @estado = svc.nStbValorCatalogoID 
	FROM StbValorCatalogo AS svc WHERE svc.nStbCatalogoID = 
	(
	SELECT sc.nStbCatalogoID
	FROM StbCatalogo AS sc
	WHERE sc.cNombre = 'EstadoSolicitudPrestamo'
	) AND  svc.cCodigoInterno = '5'
	
	
	IF @estado > 0
	BEGIN
		UPDATE ScrCredito
		SET    nStbEstadoSolicitudID     = @estado
		WHERE  nScrSolicitudID           = @creditoID
	END
		
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrDatosPrestamoConPagosRealizados]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrDatosPrestamoConPagosRealizados] @creditoId INT
AS
SELECT sc.nScrSolicitudID SOICITUDID,
	   sr.cDescripcion RUBRO,
	   MIN(stp.dFechaPago) FECHAINICIA,
	   MAX(stp.dFechaPago) FECHAFIN,
	   srd.nTasaInteres INTERES,	   
	   (srd.nPlazo / sfp.nPlazoMeses) NOPAGOS,
	   srd.nPlazo PLAZO,
	   sc.nMontoApruebaC MONTOAPROBADO,
	   SUM(stp.nMontoPagado) MONTOPAGADO	   	   
FROM ScrCredito AS sc
	JOIN StbRubroDetalle AS srd
		ON srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
	JOIN StbRubro AS sr
		ON sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
	JOIN ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stp
		ON stp.nScrSolicitudID = sc.nScrSolicitudID
	JOIN ScrPagoCuota AS spc
		ON spc.nScrSolicitudID = stp.nScrSolicitudID			
	JOIN ScrPagoCuotaDetalle AS spcd
		ON spcd.nScrPagoCuotaID = spc.nScrPagoCuotaID
		AND spcd.nScrTablaproyeccionPagoID = stp.nScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamicaID
	JOIN StbFrecuenciaPagos AS sfp
		ON sfp.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID = srd.nStbFrecuenciaPagoID
WHERE sc.nScrSolicitudID = @creditoId
		AND spc.nActivo = 255		
GROUP BY sc.nScrSolicitudID,
		 sr.cDescripcion,
		 srd.nTasaInteres,
		 sfp.nPlazoMeses,
	     sfp.nPagosAnios,
	     srd.nPlazo,
	     sc.nMontoApruebaC		
	     
	     
	     
	     
	     

GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[uspScrEliminarRolesPorCuenta] 
	@cuentaID INT
AS
BEGIN
	
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    DELETE 
    FROM SsgCuentaRol
    WHERE objCuentaID = @cuentaID
   
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrEstadoDesembolso]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrEstadoDesembolso] @tipoEstado VARCHAR(10), @desembolsoID INT
AS

DECLARE @estado INT

BEGIN
	
	SELECT @estado = svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
	FROM   StbValorCatalogo AS svc
	WHERE  svc.nStbCatalogoID = (
	           SELECT sc.nStbCatalogoID
	           FROM   StbCatalogo AS sc
	           WHERE  sc.cNombre = 'EstadoPagoDesembolso'
	       )
	       AND svc.cCodigoInterno = CASE 
	                                     WHEN @tipoEstado = 'AUTORIZAR' THEN 
	                                          '02'
	                                     ELSE '03' END

	IF @estado > 0
	BEGIN
		UPDATE ScrDesembolso
		SET    nStbEstadoDesembolsoID    = @estado
		WHERE  nScrDesembolsoID           = @desembolsoID
	END
		
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrFiadoresConPrestamoActivo]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[uspScrFiadoresConPrestamoActivo] @PersonaId INT
AS
BEGIN
	
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

    SELECT sf.*
    FROM StbFiador AS sf
		JOIN StbPersona AS sp
			ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sf.nStbPersonaID
		JOIN ScrCredito AS sc
			ON sc.nScrSolicitudID = sf.nStbSolicitudID
    WHERE sc.nStbEstadoSolicitudID IN
		(
			SELECT svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
			FROM StbValorCatalogo AS svc
			WHERE svc.nStbCatalogoID = (SELECT TOP 1 sc2.nStbCatalogoID
			                            FROM StbCatalogo AS sc2
			                            WHERE sc2.cNombre = 'EstadoSolicitudPrestamo')	
					AND svc.cCodigoInterno IN ('1','2','7')			                         
		)
		AND sf.nStbPersonaID = @PersonaId
    
END

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrListadoFiadores]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrListadoFiadores]
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

SELECT	sf.nStbFiadorID fiadorID,
		sf.nStbPersonaID personaID,
		isnull(sp.cNombre1,'') + ' ' + 
		isnull(sp.cNombre2,'') + ' ' + 
		isnull(sp.cApellido1,'') +' ' + 
		isnull(sp.cApellido2,'') fiadorName,
		sm.sNombre municipio,
		sf.cLugarTrabajo lugarTrabajo,
		pu.cDescripcion puesto,
		sf.cFuenteIngresos observacion,		
		svc.cDescripcion parentesco,
		CASE WHEN sf.nEstado = 0 THEN 'Inactivo' ELSE 'Activo' END estado
FROM StbFiador AS sf
		JOIN StbPersona AS sp
		    ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sf.nStbPersonaID	  
		JOIN StbMunicipio AS sm
			ON sm.nStbMunicipioID = sp.nStbMunicipioID
		LEFT JOIN StbValorCatalogo AS svc
			ON svc.nStbValorCatalogoID = sf.nStbParentesco
		LEFT JOIN StbValorCatalogo AS pu
			ON pu.nStbValorCatalogoID = sf.nStbPuesto
			

GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrNumeroPagosPrestamo] @creditoId INT
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

SELECT COUNT(spc.nScrPagoCuotaID) cuotas 
FROM ScrPagoCuota AS spc
WHERE spc.nScrSolicitudID = @creditoId
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrPagosCuotasPrestamo]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO



CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrPagosCuotasPrestamo] @creditoId INT
AS

SELECT T0.PAGOID,
       T0.SOLICITUDID,
       T0.FECHAPAGO,
       T0.NUMERODOCUMENTO,
       T0.TABLAPAGOID,
       T0.NUMEROCUOTA,
       T0.PRINCIPAL,
       T0.INTERES,
       T0.MORA,
       T0.MANTENIMIENTO,
       T0.TOTAL
FROM   (
           SELECT spc.nScrPagoCuotaID      PAGOID,
                  spc.nScrSolicitudID      SOLICITUDID,
                  spc.dFechaPago           FECHAPAGO,
                  spc.cNumeroDocumento     NUMERODOCUMENTO,
                  /*spcd.nScrTablaproyeccionPagoID*/ 0 TABLAPAGOID,
                  CAST(COUNT(spcd.nNumeroCuota) AS TINYINT) NUMEROCUOTA,
                  SUM(spcd.nMontoPrincipal) PRINCIPAL,
                  SUM(spcd.nMontoInteres) INTERES,
                  SUM(spcd.nMontoMoraPrincipal) MORA,
                  SUM(spcd.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal) MANTENIMIENTO,
                  --spc.nMontoPago TOTAL    
                  SUM(
                      ISNULL(spcd.nMontoPrincipal, 0.00) +
                      ISNULL(spcd.nMontoInteres, 0.00) +
                      ISNULL(spcd.nMontoMoraPrincipal, 0.00) +
                      ISNULL(spcd.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal, 0.00)
                  )                        TOTAL
           FROM   ScrPagoCuota          AS spc
                  JOIN ScrPagoCuotaDetalle AS spcd
                       ON  spcd.nScrPagoCuotaID = spc.nScrPagoCuotaID
                  JOIN ScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamica AS stp
                       ON  stp.nScrTablaproyeccionPagoDinamicaID = spcd.nScrTablaproyeccionPagoID
           WHERE  spc.nActivo = 255
                  AND stp.nScrSolicitudID = @creditoId
           GROUP BY
                  spc.nScrPagoCuotaID,
                  spc.nScrSolicitudID,
                  spc.dFechaPago,
                  spc.cNumeroDocumento
       ) T0
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrReciboPago]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrReciboPago]	@PAGOID INT
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

SELECT	spc.nScrPagoCuotaID						CUOTAID,
		spc.cNumeroDocumento					NORECIBO,
		isnull(sp.cNombre1,'') + ' ' + 
		isnull(sp.cNombre2,'') + ' ' + 
		isnull(sp.cApellido1,'') +' ' + 
		isnull(sp.cApellido2,'')				CLIENTE,
		spc.nMontoPago							MONTOPAGADO,
		UPPER(sm.cDescripcion)					MONEDA,
		spc.cConceptoPago						CONCEPTO, 
		spc2.nMontoTCambio						TIPOCAMBIO,
		sum(spcd.nMontoPrincipal)				PRINCIPAL, 
		sum(spcd.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal)	MANTENIMIENTO,
		sum(spcd.nMontoInteres)					INTERES,
		spc.dFechaPago							FECHAPAGO,
		sc.nNumeroSolicitud						NOPRESTAMO,
		sr.cDescripcion							RUBRO,
		ts.N_SALDO_TOTAL						SALDO,
		(SELECT [dbo].[FN_CONVIERTE_NUMEROS_LETRAS](spc.nMontoPago)) MONTOLETRAS,
		svc.cDescripcion						FONDO	
FROM ScrPagoCuota AS spc
	JOIN ScrPagoCuotaDetalle AS spcd
		ON spcd.nScrPagoCuotaID = spc.nScrPagoCuotaID
	JOIN ScrCredito AS sc
		ON sc.nScrSolicitudID = spc.nScrSolicitudID
	JOIN StbCliente AS sc2
		ON sc2.nStbClienteID = sc.nStbClienteID
	JOIN StbPersona AS sp
		ON sp.nStbPersonaID = sc2.nStbPersonaID
	JOIN StbParidadCambiaria AS spc2
		ON spc2.nStbParidadCambiariaID = spc.nStbParidadCambiariaID
	JOIN StbMoneda AS sm
		ON sm.nStbMonedaID = spc.nStbMonedaID
	JOIN StbRubroDetalle AS srd
		ON srd.nStbRubroDetalleID = sc.nStbRubroDetalleID
	JOIN StbRubro AS sr
		ON sr.nStbRubroID = srd.nStbRubroID
	JOIN 
		(
			SELECT TOP 1 stcp.N_PAGO_ID,
						 stcp.N_SALDO_TOTAL
			FROM   ScrTablaControlPrestamo AS stcp
			WHERE  stcp.N_PAGO_ID = @PAGOID
			ORDER BY stcp.N_INDICE DESC 	
		) ts 
		ON ts.N_PAGO_ID = spc.nScrPagoCuotaID
	JOIN StbValorCatalogo AS svc
		ON sc.nStbFondoId = svc.nStbValorCatalogoID
WHERE spc.nScrPagoCuotaID	 = @PAGOID	
GROUP BY spc.nScrPagoCuotaID,
		 spc.cNumeroDocumento,
		 isnull(sp.cNombre1,'') + ' ' + 
		 isnull(sp.cNombre2,'') + ' ' + 
		 isnull(sp.cApellido1,'') +' ' + 
		 isnull(sp.cApellido2,''),
		 spc.nMontoPago,
		 UPPER(sm.cDescripcion),
		 spc.cConceptoPago, 
		 spc2.nMontoTCambio,
		 spc.dFechaPago,
		 sc.nNumeroSolicitud,
		 sr.cDescripcion,
		 ts.N_SALDO_TOTAL,
		 svc.cDescripcion
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspScrRptDistribucionPagoPrestamoCliente]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspScrRptDistribucionPagoPrestamoCliente] @N_SOLICITUD_ID INT,
													 @FECHA_PAGO DATETIME
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

SELECT T0.N_SOLICITUD_ID, 
	   T0.CLIENTE, 
	   T0.N_MONTO_APRUEBA, 
	   T0.DESLIZAMIENTO,
       T0.DFECHAPAGADO, 
       T0.NPLAZOMESES, 
       T0.NTASAINTERES, 
       T0.VENCE, 
       T0.FRECUENCIA,
       T0.NUMPAGOS, 
       T0.NMONTOTCAMBIO, 
       T0.RUBRO, 
       T1.N_INDICE,        
       T1.D_FECHA_CORTE, 
       T1.N_TIPO_CAMBIO, 
       T1.N_DIAS_ENTRE_FECHA, 
       T1.N_SALDO_TOTAL,
       T1.N_DESEMBOLSO_ACTUALIZADO, 
       T1.N_SALDO_AMORTIZACION,
       T1.N_MANTENIMIENTO_DEVENGADO_AM, 
       T1.N_MANTENIMIENTO_DEVENGADO_ACUMULADO_AM,
       T1.N_MANTENIMIENTO_ABONADO_AM, 
       T1.N_MANTENIMIENTO_ABONADO_ACUMULADO_AM,
       T1.N_MANTENIMIENTO_PENDIENTE_AM, 
       T1.N_MANTENIMIENTO_PENDIENTE_ACUMULADO_AM,
       T1.N_AMORTIZACION_DEVENGADA, 
       T1.N_AMORTIZACION_DEVEGADA_ACUMULADA,
       T1.N_AMORTIZACION_ABONADA, 
       T1.N_AMORTIZACION_ABONADA_ACUMULADA,
       T1.N_AMORTIZACION_PENDIENTE, 
       T1.N_AMORTIZACION_PENDIENTE_ACUMULADO,
       T1.N_INTERES_DEVENGADO, 
       T1.N_INTERES_DEVENGADO_ACUMULADO,
       T1.N_INTERES_ABONADO, 
       T1.N_INTERES_ABONADO_ACUMULADO,
       T1.N_INTERES_PENDIENTE, 
       T1.N_INTERES_PENDIENTE_ACUMULADO
FROM 
(
	SELECT  N_SOLICITUD_ID, 
			cliente CLIENTE, 
			nMontoApruebaC N_MONTO_APRUEBA, 
			deslizamiento DESLIZAMIENTO, 
			dFechaPagado DFECHAPAGADO,
			nPlazoMeses NPLAZOMESES, 
			nTasaInteres NTASAINTERES, 
			vence VENCE, 
			frecuencia FRECUENCIA, 
			NumPagos NUMPAGOS, 
			nMontoTCambio NMONTOTCAMBIO,
			rubro RUBRO 
	FROM  [dbo].[fnDatosPrestamoCliente]	(@N_SOLICITUD_ID)	
)T0
JOIN
(
	SELECT N_INDICE,
		   N_SOLICITUD_ID,
		   D_FECHA_CORTE,
		   N_TIPO_CAMBIO,
		   N_DIAS_ENTRE_FECHA,
		   N_SALDO_TOTAL,
		   N_DESEMBOLSO_ACTUALIZADO,
		   N_SALDO_AMORTIZACION,
		   N_MANTENIMIENTO_DEVENGADO_AM,
		   N_MANTENIMIENTO_DEVENGADO_ACUMULADO_AM,
		   N_MANTENIMIENTO_ABONADO_AM,
		   N_MANTENIMIENTO_ABONADO_ACUMULADO_AM, 
		   N_MANTENIMIENTO_PENDIENTE_AM,
		   N_MANTENIMIENTO_PENDIENTE_ACUMULADO_AM, 
		   N_AMORTIZACION_DEVENGADA,
		   N_AMORTIZACION_DEVEGADA_ACUMULADA, 
		   N_AMORTIZACION_ABONADA,
		   N_AMORTIZACION_ABONADA_ACUMULADA, 
		   N_AMORTIZACION_PENDIENTE,
		   N_AMORTIZACION_PENDIENTE_ACUMULADO,
		   N_INTERES_DEVENGADO, N_INTERES_DEVENGADO_ACUMULADO, N_INTERES_ABONADO,
		   N_INTERES_ABONADO_ACUMULADO, N_INTERES_PENDIENTE,
		   N_INTERES_PENDIENTE_ACUMULADO	   
	FROM  DBO.FN_DISTRIBUCION_PAGO(@FECHA_PAGO, @N_SOLICITUD_ID)	
	WHERE N_PAGO_ID IS NULL
)	T1
ON T0.N_SOLICITUD_ID = T1.N_SOLICITUD_ID												 
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspSsgServicioUsuarioCuentaAplicacion]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[uspSsgServicioUsuarioCuentaAplicacion] @cuentaId INT, @aplicacionId INT
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

SELECT su.SsgServicioUsuarioID,
       su.CodInterno,
       su.Nombre,
       su.Descripcion,
       su.UsuarioCreacion,
       su.FechaCreacion,
       su.UsuarioModificacion,
       su.FechaModificacion,
       su.objModuloID
FROM   SsgAccion a
       JOIN SsgServicioUsuario AS su
            ON  su.SsgServicioUsuarioID = a.objServicioUsuarioID
       JOIN SsgModulo AS sm
			ON sm.SsgModuloID = su.objModuloID
WHERE  SsgAccionID IN (SELECT objAccionID
                       FROM   SsgRolAccion
                              INNER JOIN SsgRol
                                   ON  SsgRolAccion.objRolID = SsgRol.SsgRolID
                              INNER JOIN SsgCuentaRol
                                   ON  SsgRol.SsgRolID = SsgCuentaRol.objRolID
                       WHERE  SsgCuentaRol.objCuentaID = @cuentaId) --67
       AND sm.objAplicacionID = @aplicacionId
GROUP BY
       su.SsgServicioUsuarioID,
       su.CodInterno,
       su.Nombre,
       su.Descripcion,
       su.UsuarioCreacion,
       su.FechaCreacion,
       su.UsuarioModificacion,
       su.FechaModificacion,
       su.objModuloID 
       

GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspStbEmpresaDatos]
AS

SET NOCOUNT ON

SELECT se.nStbEmpresaID,
       se.cNombreInstitucion	cNombreEmpresa,
       se.cNombreCorto			cNombreCortoEmpresa,
       se.cRazonSocial			cRazonSocialEmpresa,
       se.cDireccion			cDireccionEmpresa,
       se.cNumeroRUC			cNumeroRUCEmpresa,
       se.cNumeroPatronal		cNumeroPatronalEmpresa,
       se.bLogo					bLogoEmpresa
FROM   StbEmpresa AS se

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[uspTablaProyeccionPorCredito]    Script Date: 19/05/2026 16:53:19 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO


CREATE PROC [dbo].[uspTablaProyeccionPorCredito] @N_CREDITO_ID INT
AS

SELECT	stp.nScrTablaproyeccionPagoID, 
		stp.nScrSolicitudID, 
		stp.nNumeroCuota,
		stp.dFechaPago, 
		stp.nMontoPrincipal, 
		stp.nMontoPrincipalAbonado,
		stp.nMontoMantenimientoPrincipal, 
		stp.nMontoMantenimientoAbonadoPrincipal,
		stp.nMontoInteres, 
		stp.nMontoInteresAbonado, 
		stp.nMontoMora,
		stp.nMontoMoraAbonado, 
		stp.nMontoMantenimientoInteres,
		stp.nMontoMantenimientoInteresAbonado, 
		stp.nMontoTotal, 
		stp.nMontoPagado,
		stp.nMontoSaldo 
FROM ScrTablaproyeccionPago AS stp
WHERE stp.nScrSolicitudID = @N_CREDITO_ID
GO
